<script>
var touchmoved;
const dropMenu1 = document.querySelector('#drop-menu-1');
const dropMenu2 = document.querySelector('#drop-menu-2');
const mobileMenus = document.querySelectorAll('.menu-mobile');

['click','ontouchstart','ontouchend','ontouchmove'].forEach(event => {

	document.addEventListener(event, function(e){
	    for (var target = e.target; target && target != this; target = target.parentNode){

	    	/* open the mobile nav from hamburger */
			if (target.matches('.header .nav-trigger')){
	        	switch(event){
	        		case 'ontouchstart': touchmoved = false; break;
	        		case 'ontouchmove': touchmoved = true; break;
	        		case 'click': case 'ontouchend': e.preventDefault();
					    if (touchmoved) return;
						setTimeout(() => {
							dropMenu1.className = 'drop-menu-mobile';
							dropMenu2.className = 'drop-menu-mobile';
						}, 500);
	        			break;
	        	}
	            break;
	        }
			/* go forward into a menu */
	        if (target.matches('.slide-menu-link')){
	        	switch(event){
	        		case 'ontouchstart': touchmoved = false; break;
	        		case 'ontouchmove': touchmoved = true; break;
	        		case 'click': case 'ontouchend': e.preventDefault();
					    if (touchmoved) return;
						let tid = target.getAttribute('data-menu');
						mobileMenus.forEach(menu => {
							menu.style.display = (menu.classList.contains(tid)) ? 'block' : 'none';
						});
						dropMenu1.className = 'drop-menu-mobile move-left';
						dropMenu2.className = 'drop-menu-mobile move-left';


						if (window.webkit && window.webkit.messageHandlers && window.webkit.messageHandlers.navigationHandler){
							webkit.messageHandlers.navigationHandler.postMessage({name: target.innerText.trim()});
						}

						if (tid === 'search-menu-mobile'){
							setTimeout(() => {
								dropMenu2.querySelector('.search-input').focus();
							}, 600);
						}
						break;
	        	}
				break;
	        }
	        /* go backwards out of a menu */
			if (target.matches('.back-menu-link')){
	        	switch(event){
	        		case 'ontouchstart': touchmoved = false; break;
	        		case 'ontouchmove': touchmoved = true; break;
	        		case 'click': case 'ontouchend': e.preventDefault();
					    if (touchmoved) return;
						dropMenu1.className = 'drop-menu-mobile move-right';
						dropMenu2.className = 'drop-menu-mobile move-right';
	        			break;
	        	}
	            break;
			}

	    }
	}, false);

});


if(typeof bootstrap == "undefined"){
    document.getElementById('bs5-script').addEventListener("load", function(e){
        // --- Makes sure tooltips are added to dynamically created elements
        new bootstrap.Tooltip(document.body, {"selector":"[data-bs-toggle=\"tooltip\"]"});
    })
} else {
    new bootstrap.Tooltip(document.body, {"selector":"[data-bs-toggle=\"tooltip\"]"});
}</script>
<script>jQuery(function ($) {
jQuery('#adp-form').yiiActiveForm([], []);
$("body").on("click", "[data-sort]", function(e){
    var newOrderField = $(this).attr("data-sort");
    if( newOrderField == $("#adpform-orderfield").val() ){
        if($("#adpform-orderdirection").val() == "4"){
            $("#adpform-orderdirection").val("3")
        } else {
            $("#adpform-orderdirection").val("4")
        }
    } else {
        $("#adpform-orderfield").val(newOrderField)
        $("#adpform-orderdirection").val($(this).attr("data-sort-dir-default"))
    }
    $("#adpform-orderfield").trigger("change")
    $("#adpform-orderdirection").trigger("change")
});
jQuery('#w0').yiiGridView({"filterUrl":"\/adp\/ppr?AdpForm%5BorderField%5D=ffnOverall\u0026AdpForm%5BorderDirection%5D=4\u0026AdpForm%5BleagueSize%5D=12\u0026AdpForm%5BleagueSize%5D=8","filterSelector":"#w0-filters input, #w0-filters select","filterOnFocusOut":true});
$('.flash.alert').prepend('<div class="gradient" />');
$(window).one('mousewheel', function(){
    setTimeout(hideFlashAlerts, 300);  
});
$(document).one('click', '[data-dismiss="alert"]', function(){
    $(this).parent().fadeOut(function(){
       $(this).remove();
    });
});
function hideFlashAlerts(){
    $('.flash.alert-success').removeClass('in');
    setTimeout(function(e){
        $('.flash.alert-success').remove();
    }, 300);
}
setTimeout(hideFlashAlerts, 0);
});</script></body>
